<center>01-安装hexo及在github上传载（linux系统）</center>

Linux：安装Hexo

参考资料

https://easyhexo.com/1-Hexo-install-and-config/1-2-install-hexo.html#%E5%AE%89%E8%A3%85-git

https://developer.aliyun.com/article/760687

https://www.bilibili.com/read/cv12633102 （写的很好）2021最全hexo搭建博客+matery美化+使用（保姆级教程）

https://github.com/blinkfox/hexo-theme-matery/blob/develop/README_CN.md （中文使用文档）

https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/DrEc8FqycC15hp2X010wxQ（羊哥的视频）

…

安装Git

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ # 安装Git
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ sudo apt-get install git-core
[sudo] jincanliu 的密码： 
正在读取软件包列表... 完成
正在分析软件包的依赖关系树     
正在读取状态信息... 完成     
注意，选中 'git' 而非 'git-core'
git 已经是最新版 (1:2.25.1-1ubuntu3.2)。
升级了 0 个软件包，新安装了 0 个软件包，要卸载 0 个软件包，有 82 个软件包未被升级。
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ git version
git version 2.25.1

安装Nodejs(版本过低可能导致hexo server无法运行)

方法一（失败）

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ # 安装Node.js    https://easyhexo.com/1-Hexo-install-and-config/1-2-install-hexo.html#%E5%AE%89%E8%A3%85-git
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ $ wget -qO- https://raw.github.com/creationix/nvm/v0.33.11/install.sh | sh
$：未找到命令
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ wget -qO- https://raw.github.com/creationix/nvm/v0.33.11/install.sh | sh
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ # 安装完成后，重启终端并执行下列命令即可安装 Node.js。
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ nvm install stable

Command 'nvm' not found, but there are 13 similar ones.

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ # 怀疑是目录中文问题
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/桌面$ cd
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ wget -qO- https://raw.github.com/creationix/nvm/v0.33.11/install.sh | sh
=> nvm is already installed in /home/jincanliu/.nvm, trying to update using git
=> => Compressing and cleaning up git repository

=> nvm source string already in /home/jincanliu/.profile
=> bash_completion source string already in /home/jincanliu/.profile
=> Close and reopen your terminal to start using nvm or run the following to use it now:

export NVM_DIR="$HOME/.nvm"
[ -s "$NVM_DIR/nvm.sh" ] && \. "$NVM_DIR/nvm.sh"  # This loads nvm
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ nvm install stable

Command 'nvm' not found, but there are 13 similar ones.

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # 怀疑是没有更新.bashrc
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ source ~/.bashrc
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ nvm install stable

Command 'nvm' not found, but there are 13 similar ones.

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # 检查nvm版本，到底安装上没
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ nvm --version

Command 'nvm' not found, but there are 13 similar ones.

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # 怀疑是.bash_profile没更新（http://tiaocaoer.com/blog/nvm.html）
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ source ~/.bash_profile
bash: /home/jincanliu/.bash_profile: 没有那个文件或目录
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # curl安装nvm
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$  curl https://raw.github.com/creationix/nvm/v0.33.11/install.sh | sh
  % Total    % Received % Xferd  Average Speed   Time    Time     Time  Current
                                 Dload  Upload   Total   Spent    Left  Speed
  0     0    0     0    0     0      0      0 --:--:-- --:--:-- --:--:--     0
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ nvm

Command 'nvm' not found, but there are 13 similar ones.

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ #------ wget和curl安装失败，尝试下载安装程序进行安装。（下载地址：https://nodejs.org/en/）
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # 下载包所在地址：/home/jincanliu/BaiduNetdiskWorkspace/Program_setup
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # node-v16.13.1-linux-x64.tar.xz
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ # 安装tar.xz文件（https://ubuntuqa.com/article/9015.html）
(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~$ tar xvfJ /home/jincanliu/BaiduNetdiskWorkspace/Program_setup
tar (child): /home/jincanliu/BaiduNetdiskWorkspace/Program_setup：无法 read: 是一个目录
tar (child): 处于磁带的起点，现在退出

xz： (stdin): 无法识别文件格式

     sudo apt-get install gcc g++ make

     echo "deb [signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/yarnkey.gpg] https://dl.yarnpkg.com/debian stable main" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/yarn.list
     sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install yarn

(base) jincanliu@jincanliu-Z390-UD:~/BaiduNetdiskWorkspace/Liu-Jincan.github.io$ cat _config.yml 

# Hexo Configuration
## Docs: https://hexo.io/docs/configuration.html
## Source: https://github.com/hexojs/hexo/

# Site
title: Hexo
subtitle: ''
description: ''
keywords:
author: John Doe
language: en
timezone: ''

# URL
## Set your site url here. For example, if you use GitHub Page, set url as 'https://username.github.io/project'
url: http://example.com
permalink: :year/:month/:day/:title/
permalink_defaults:
pretty_urls:
  trailing_index: true # Set to false to remove trailing 'index.html' from permalinks
  trailing_html: true # Set to false to remove trailing '.html' from permalinks

# Directory
source_dir: source
public_dir: public
tag_dir: tags
archive_dir: archives
category_dir: categories
code_dir: downloads/code
i18n_dir: :lang
skip_render:

# Writing
new_post_name: :title.md # File name of new posts
default_layout: post
titlecase: false # Transform title into titlecase
external_link:
  enable: true # Open external links in new tab
  field: site # Apply to the whole site
  exclude: ''
filename_case: 0
render_drafts: false
post_asset_folder: false
relative_link: false
future: true
highlight:
  enable: true
  line_number: true
  auto_detect: false
  tab_replace: ''
  wrap: true
  hljs: false
prismjs:
  enable: false
  preprocess: true
  line_number: true
  tab_replace: ''

# Home page setting
# path: Root path for your blogs index page. (default = '')
# per_page: Posts displayed per page. (0 = disable pagination)
# order_by: Posts order. (Order by date descending by default)
index_generator:
  path: ''
  per_page: 10
  order_by: -date

# Category & Tag
default_category: uncategorized
category_map:
tag_map:

# Metadata elements
## https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/meta
meta_generator: true

# Date / Time format
## Hexo uses Moment.js to parse and display date
## You can customize the date format as defined in
## http://momentjs.com/docs/#/displaying/format/
date_format: YYYY-MM-DD
time_format: HH:mm:ss
## updated_option supports 'mtime', 'date', 'empty'
updated_option: 'mtime'

# Pagination
## Set per_page to 0 to disable pagination
per_page: 10
pagination_dir: page

# Include / Exclude file(s)
## include:/exclude: options only apply to the 'source/' folder
include:
exclude:
ignore:

# Extensions
## Plugins: https://hexo.io/plugins/
## Themes: https://hexo.io/themes/
theme: landscape

# Deployment
## Docs: https://hexo.io/docs/one-command-deployment
deploy:
  type: git
  repo: https://github.com/Liu-Jincan/Liu-Jincan.github.io.git
  branch: main
